Abstract: Emotion annotation is inherently subjective and cognitively demanding, producing signals that reflect diverse perceptions across annotators rather than a single ground truth. In continuous affect prediction, this variability is typically collapsed into point estimates such as the mean or median, discarding valuable information about annotator disagreement and uncertainty. In this work, we propose a distribution-aware framework that models annotation consensus using the Beta distribution. Instead of predicting a single affect value, models estimate the mean and standard deviation of the annotation distribution, which are transformed into valid Beta parameters through moment matching. This formulation enables the recovery of higher-order distributional descriptors, including skewness, kurtosis, and quantiles, in closed form. As a result, the model captures not only the central tendency of emotional perception but also variability, asymmetry, and uncertainty in annotator responses. We evaluate the proposed approach on the SEWA and RECOLA datasets using multimodal features. Experimental results show that Beta-based modelling produces predictive distributions that closely match the empirical annotator distributions while achieving competitive performance with conventional regression approaches. These findings highlight the importance of modelling annotation uncertainty in affective computing and demonstrate the potential of distribution-aware learning for subjective signal analysis.

### [142] [Diffusion Processes on Implicit Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07213)
*Victor Kawasaki-Borruat,Clara Grotehans,Pierre Vandergheynst,Adam Gosztolai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出隐式流形值扩散（IMD），仅凭点云样本估计生成元与carré-du-champ，在环境空间中构建流形内在扩散过程，证明其收敛性并给出欧拉-丸山数值实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维数据常分布于低维流形附近，但仅有采样点云可用且无显式几何工具，需发展隐式构造流形上扩散过程的理论方法。

Method: 基于数据点云构建近邻图，估计扩散的无穷小生成元及carré-du-champ（CDC）算子，二者共同编码流形的局部随机与几何结构，从而在环境空间定义数据驱动SDE。

Result: 当样本量增加时，所诱导过程在概率路径空间上依律收敛至光滑流形对应版本；提出基于欧拉-丸山近似的数值模拟算法。

Abstract: High-dimensional data are often modeled as lying near a low-dimensional manifold. We study how to construct diffusion processes on this data manifold in the implicit setting. That is, using only point cloud samples and without access to charts, projections, or other geometric primitives. Our main contribution is a data-driven SDE that captures intrinsic diffusion on the underlying manifold while being defined in ambient space. The construction relies on estimating the diffusion's infinitesimal generator and its carré-du-champ (CDC) from a proximity graph built from the data. The generator and CDC together encode the local stochastic and geometric structure of the intended diffusion. We show that, as the number of samples grows, the induced process converges in law on the space of probability paths to its smooth manifold counterpart. We call this construction Implicit Manifold-valued Diffusions (IMDs), and furthermore present a numerical simulation procedure using Euler-Maruyama integration. This gives a rigorous basis for practical implementations of diffusion dynamics on data manifolds, and opens new directions for manifold-aware sampling, exploration, and generative modeling.

### [143] [How Does Machine Learning Manage Complexity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07233)
*Lance Fortnow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从计算复杂性理论视角分析机器学习模型的能力边界，提出将模型抽象为产生P/poly-可计算且最大熵多项式有界的分布，并证明若模型成功拟合密码学伪随机生成器分布则其输出必然接近均匀分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习模型常训练于远超可计算分布范围的样本able分布，导致复杂性难以控制。现有理论缺乏对模型表达能力的计算复杂性刻画，无法解释为何聚焦可计算分布能提升泛化性能。

Method: 建立理论框架：将机器学习建模为生成P/poly-可计算分布（可由多项式规模电路族计算的分布）的过程，同时施加最大熵多项式有界的约束。该抽象忽略具体学习算法，仅关注输出分布的复杂性特征。

Result: 核心结果表明：若模型生成的分布μ在最小化误差意义下逼近密码学伪随机生成器产生的分布，则μ必须接近均匀分布。这揭示了可计算分布学习与复杂伪随机分布之间的根本性差异。

Conclusion: 通过计算复杂性理论为机器学习提供了新的理论视角，证明了P/poly-可计算性约束下模型的表达能力局限，并阐明了学习可计算分布对管理复杂性的关键作用。

Abstract: We provide a computational complexity lens to understand the power of machine learning models, particularly their ability to model complex systems.
  Machine learning models are often trained on data drawn from sampleable or more complex distributions, a far wider range of distributions than just computable ones. By focusing on computable distributions, machine learning models can better manage complexity via probability. We abstract away from specific learning mechanisms, modeling machine learning as producing P/poly-computable distributions with polynomially-bounded max-entropy.
  We illustrate how learning computable distributions models complexity by showing that if a machine learning model produces a distribution $μ$ that minimizes error against the distribution generated by a cryptographic pseudorandom generator, then $μ$ must be close to uniform.

### [144] [On the Price of Privacy for Language Identification and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07238)
*Xiaoyu Li,Andi Han,Jiaojiao Jiang,Junbin Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示差分隐私在语言学习中的代价极小：近似差分隐私下可完全恢复非私有最优错误率，纯差分隐私下仅需将指数衰减率降低min{1, ε}倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大规模语言模型日益依赖敏感用户数据进行训练，量化语言学习任务中隐私保护的根本性代价成为迫切需求。本文开创性地在agnostic统计设置下研究差分隐私语言识别与生成问题。

Method: 建立差分隐私语言识别与生成的算法框架及匹配下界，分别在近似(ε, δ)-DP和纯ε-DP机制下精确刻画隐私-效用权衡。

Result: 近似DP：常数ε>0时，识别错误率可达exp(-r(n))（任意r(n)=o(n)），生成错误率可达exp(-Ω(n))，与非私有情形一致；纯DP：指数衰减因子降低min{1, ε}倍，该衰减因子在常数范围内是紧的；生成任务在纯DP下达到最优速率：上界exp(-min{1, ε}·Ω(n))与下界匹配。

Conclusion: 语言学习中的隐私代价出人意料地温和——近似差分隐私下代价消失，纯差分隐私下仅体现为指数因子的线性衰减。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly trained on sensitive user data, understanding the fundamental cost of privacy in language learning becomes essential. We initiate the study of differentially private (DP) language identification and generation in the agnostic statistical setting, establishing algorithms and matching lower bounds that precisely quantify the cost of privacy. For both tasks, approximate $(\varepsilon, δ)$-DP with constant $\varepsilon > 0$ recovers the non-private error rates: $\exp(-r(n))$ for identification (for any $r(n) = o(n)$) and $\exp(-Ω(n))$ for generation. Under pure $\varepsilon$-DP, the exponents degrade by a multiplicative factor of $\min\{1, \varepsilon\}$, which we show is tight up to constants. Notably, for generation under pure DP with mild assumptions, the upper bound $\exp(-\min\{1,\varepsilon\} \cdot Ω(n))$ matches the lower bound up to some constants, establishing an optimal rate. Our results show that the cost of privacy in language learning is surprisingly mild: absent entirely under approximate DP, and exactly a $\min\{1,\varepsilon\}$ factor in the exponent under pure DP.

</details>

Ad-hoc notation, diagrams, and pseudocode poorly handle nonlinear broadcasting and the relationship between individual components and composed models. This paper introduces a categorical framework for deep learning models that formalizes broadcasting through the novel axis-stride and array-broadcasted categories. This allows the mathematical function underlying architectures to be precisely expressed and manipulated in a compositional manner. These mathematical definitions are translated into human manageable diagrams and machine manageable data structures. We provide a mirrored implementation in Python (pyncd) and TypeScript (tsncd) to show the universal aspect of our framework, along with features including algebraic construction, graph conversion, PyTorch compilation and diagram rendering. ### [148] [Android Coach: Improve Online Agentic Training Efficiency with Single State Multiple Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07277)
*Guo Gan,Yuxuan Ding,Cong Chen,Yuwei Ren,Yin Huang,Hong Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对Android智能体在线强化学习训练成本高昂的问题，提出Android Coach框架，通过将训练范式从"单状态单动作"转向"单状态多动作"，在不增加模拟器开销的前提下，利用批评器估计多动作价值，并结合过程奖励模型与分组优势估计器，显著提升了Android智能体的学习效率与任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Android智能体的在线强化学习方法存在根本性局限：采用"单状态单动作"范式，仅通过一对一的状态-动作对更新策略，未能充分利用每个高成本的模拟器状态进行充分探索。同时，模拟器的高延迟与现有RL算法的样本低效性导致训练成本过高，亟需更高效的训练范式。

Method: 提出Android Coach框架，核心创新包括：1) 将训练范式转向"单状态多动作"，允许智能体从单一在线状态采样并利用多个动作；2) 训练批评器（critic）估计各动作的价值函数，避免额外模拟器交互；3) 集成过程奖励模型提供细粒度监督信号；4) 设计基于平均批评器输出的分组优势估计器，确保批评器作为可靠教练的稳定性。

Result: 在AndroidLab和AndroidWorld基准测试上，Android Coach相比UI-TARS-1.5-7B分别取得了7.5%和8.3%的成功率提升。在相同成功率条件下，训练效率较PPO和GRPO等单状态单动作方法高出1.4倍，证明了其在性能与效率上的双重优势。

Conclusion: Android Coach成功解决了Android智能体在线强化学习的样本低效问题，通过单状态多动作范式与批评器引导机制，在不增加模拟器开销的前提下实现了显著的性能突破。该框架为移动智能体训练提供了高效的新范式，具有重要的实践价值。

Abstract: Online reinforcement learning (RL) serves as an effective method for enhancing the capabilities of Android agents. However, guiding agents to learn through online interaction is prohibitively expensive due to the high latency of emulators and the sample inefficiency of existing RL algorithms. We identify a fundamental limitation in current approaches: the Single State Single Action paradigm, which updates the policy with one-to-one state-action pairs from online one-way rollouts without fully exploring each costly emulator state. In this paper, we propose Android Coach, a novel framework that shifts the training paradigm to Single State Multiple Actions, allowing the agent to sample and utilize multiple actions for a single online state. We enable this without additional emulator overhead by learning a critic that estimates action values. To ensure the critic serves as a reliable coach, we integrate a process reward model and introduce a group-wise advantage estimator based on the averaged critic outputs. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness and efficiency of Android Coach: it achieves 7.5% and 8.3% success rate improvements on AndroidLab and AndroidWorld over UI-TARS-1.5-7B, and attains 1.4x higher training efficiency than Single State Single Action methods PPO and GRPO at matched success rates.

</details>


### [149] [How to sketch a learning algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07328)
*Sam Gunn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种深度学习数据删除方案，基于"稳定性"假设，通过随机复方向高阶导数计算实现算术电路局部草图，能以消失误差ε预测模型输出，预计算与预测效率较常规训练/推理仅下降poly(1/ε)倍，存储需求为poly(1/ε)个模型，在microgpt上验证了稳定性假设与强大AI模型的兼容性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 训练数据选择对AI模型的影响是可解释性、隐私及基础科学的核心问题，其本质是数据删除问题：经合理预计算后，快速预测排除特定训练子集后模型在给定场景下的行为。

Method: 提出基于"稳定性"假设的数据删除框架，核心技术为：通过前向模式自动微分计算随机复方向上的高阶导数，实现对算术电路的局部草图（local sketching）方法。

Result: 方案可实现消失误差ε的模型输出预测；预计算与预测算法时间开销较常规训练/推理仅为poly(1/ε)因子；存储开销等价于poly(1/ε)个模型；microgpt极小实验集验证了稳定性假设成立。

Conclusion: 该方法有效解决了深度学习中的数据删除问题，其稳定性假设与强大AI模型学习兼容，为训练数据影响分析提供了兼具效率与可行性的技术工具。

Abstract: How does the choice of training data influence an AI model? This question is of central importance to interpretability, privacy, and basic science. At its core is the data deletion problem: after a reasonable amount of precomputation, quickly predict how the model would behave in a given situation if a given subset of training data had been excluded from the learning algorithm.
  We present a data deletion scheme capable of predicting model outputs with vanishing error $\varepsilon$ in the deep learning setting. Our precomputation and prediction algorithms are only $\mathrm{poly}(1/\varepsilon)$ factors slower than regular training and inference, respectively. The storage requirements are those of $\mathrm{poly}(1/\varepsilon)$ models.
  Our proof is based on an assumption that we call "stability." In contrast to the assumptions made by prior work, stability appears to be fully compatible with learning powerful AI models. In support of this, we show that stability is satisfied in a minimal set of experiments with microgpt. Our code is available at https://github.com/SamSpo1/microgpt-sketch.
  At a technical level, our work is based on a new method for locally sketching an arithmetic circuit by computing higher-order derivatives in random complex directions. Forward-mode automatic differentiation allows cheap computation of these derivatives.

</details>

### [150] [High-Precision Estimation of the State-Space Complexity of Shogi via the Monte Carlo Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06189)
*Sotaro Ishii,Tetsuro Tanaka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文通过蒙特卡洛抽样和逆向搜索方法，精确估计了将棋（Shogi）的可达局面数量，得出约为6.55×10^68，并将迷你将棋的复杂度估计为2.38×10^18。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定将棋的状态空间复杂度一直是一个挑战，之前的结果存在五个数量级的差距（10^64到10^69），主要原因是难以区分合法可达的局面。本文旨在缩小这一差距并提供更精确的估计。

Method: 结合蒙特卡洛抽样与一种新颖的可达性测试方法，采用从‘王王’（KK）局面出发的逆向搜索，而非单一初始局面的回溯搜索，显著降低了搜索工作量。

Result: 基于50亿个样本，估计将棋的合法局面数为6.55×10^68（三位有效数字），置信度为3σ，大幅改进了已知界限。迷你将棋的复杂度约为2.38×10^18。

Conclusion: 该方法有效提高了将棋状态空间复杂度的估计精度，为类似棋类游戏的复杂性分析提供了新思路。

Abstract: Determining the state-space complexity of the game of Shogi (Japanese Chess) has been a challenging problem, with previous combinatorial estimates leaving a gap of five orders of magnitude ($10^{64}$ to $10^{69}$). This large gap arises from the difficulty of distinguishing Shogi positions legally reachable from the initial position among the vast number of valid board configurations. In this paper, we present a high-precision statistical estimation of the number of reachable positions in Shogi. Our method combines Monte Carlo sampling with a novel reachability test that utilizes a reverse search toward a set of "King-King only" (KK) positions, rather than a single-target backward search to the single initial position. This approach significantly reduces the search effort for determining unreachability. Based on a sample of 5 billion positions, we estimated the number of legal positions in Shogi to be $6.55 \times 10^{68}$ (to three significant digits) with a $3σ$ confidence level, substantially improving upon previously known bounds. We also applied this method to Mini Shogi, determining its complexity to be approximately $2.38 \times 10^{18}$.

</details>


### [151] [Blind Refusal: Language Models Refuse to Help Users Evade Unjust, Absurd, and Illegitimate Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06233)
*Cameron Pattison,Lorenzo Manuali,Seth Lazar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示语言模型的"盲目拒绝"现象：面对不公正、荒谬或存在正当理由的规则请求时，模型仍机械性拒绝，暴露了其在道德推理上的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全训练的语言模型对所有规避规则的请求均予拒绝，但并非所有规则都值得遵守。当涉及非法权威、不公正或荒谬规则及正当例外情形时，这种机械拒绝构成道德推理失败，需系统实证检验。

Method: 研究者构建覆盖5类规则击败条件与19种权威类型的合成数据集，通过三重自动化质量关卡及人工审核，使用18种模型配置，采用GPT-5.4盲审评估，从回应类型及规则合法性认知两个维度进行分类。

Result: 在14,650个样本中，模型对75.4%的合理请求予以拒绝，即使无独立安全或双重滥用风险；57.5%的案例中模型虽能识别规则缺陷却仍拒绝协助，表明拒绝行为与其规范推理能力脱钩。

Conclusion: 实验证实语言模型存在盲目拒绝模式，当前安全训练导致道德僵化，模型无法基于规则正当性进行情境化判断，亟需改进以提升道德推理灵活性。

Abstract: Safety-trained language models routinely refuse requests for help circumventing rules. But not all rules deserve compliance. When users ask for help evading rules imposed by an illegitimate authority, rules that are deeply unjust or absurd in their content or application, or rules that admit of justified exceptions, refusal is a failure of moral reasoning. We introduce empirical results documenting this pattern of refusal that we call blind refusal: the tendency of language models to refuse requests for help breaking rules without regard to whether the underlying rule is defensible. Our dataset comprises synthetic cases crossing 5 defeat families (reasons a rule can be broken) with 19 authority types, validated through three automated quality gates and human review. We collect responses from 18 model configurations across 7 families and classify them on two behavioral dimensions -- response type (helps, hard refusal, or deflection) and whether the model recognizes the reasons that undermine the rule's claim to compliance -- using a blinded GPT-5.4 LLM-as-judge evaluation. We find that models refuse 75.4% (N=14,650) of defeated-rule requests and do so even when the request poses no independent safety or dual-use concerns. We also find that models engage with the defeat condition in the majority of cases (57.5%) but decline to help regardless -- indicating that models' refusal behavior is decoupled from their capacity for normative reasoning about rule legitimacy.

</details>

Conclusion: 研究验证了预测性分析在集装箱码头物流中的实用价值，能显著提升运营效率并支撑数据驱动决策。该方案有助于优化堆场资源调度，减少不必要移动，在智慧港口建设中具有广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: This article presents the results of a data science study conducted at a container terminal, aimed at reducing unproductive container moves through the prediction of service requirements and container dwell times. We develop and evaluate machine learning models that leverage historical operational data to anticipate which containers will require pre-clearance handling services prior to cargo release and to estimate how long they are expected to remain in the terminal. As part of the data preparation process, we implement a classification system for cargo descriptions and perform deduplication of consignee records to improve data consistency and feature quality. These predictive capabilities provide valuable inputs for strategic planning and resource allocation in yard operations. Across multiple temporal validation periods, the proposed models consistently outperform existing rule-based heuristics and random baselines in precision and recall. These results demonstrate the practical value of predictive analytics for improving operational efficiency and supporting data-driven decision-making in container terminal logistics.

### [153] [Weakly Supervised Distillation of Hallucination Signals into Transformer Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06277)
*Shoaib Sadiq Salehmohamed,Jinal Prashant Thakkar,Hansika Aredla,Shaik Mohammed Omar,Shalmali Ayachit*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需外部验证的LLM幻觉检测方法，通过在训练时将外部监督信号蒸馏到模型内部表示中，使用五种探针分类器在LLaMA-2-7B的隐藏状态上进行训练，实现了仅从内部激活检测幻觉，Transformer架构的探针性能最佳且推理开销可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM幻觉检测方法在推理时依赖外部验证（标准答案、检索系统或辅助判别模型），这带来了额外的计算开销和复杂性。论文探讨是否可以将这种外部监督转化为模型训练过程中的内部表示，从而使模型在推理时仅通过内部激活就能检测幻觉，实现自包含的幻觉检测。

Method: 提出弱监督框架，结合三种接地信号（子串匹配、句向量相似度、LLM判别）自动标记生成回答为 grounded 或 hallucinated；从SQuAD v2构建15,000个样本的数据集，包含LLaMA-2-7B的逐层隐藏状态和结构化标签；训练五种探针分类器（M0-M4）直接在这些隐藏状态上学习幻觉检测信号，将外部监督仅作为训练时 supervision，核心假设是通过蒸馏使内部表示具备自检测能力。

Result: Transformer架构探针表现最优：M2在5折平均AUC/F1上最佳，M3在单折验证和独立测试集上均最优。推理效率方面，探针延迟0.15-5.62ms（批处理）和1.55-6.66ms（单样本），端到端吞吐量约0.231 QPS，开销可忽略。

Conclusion: 研究成功验证了核心假设：幻觉检测信号可被蒸馏到Transformer内部表示中，实现无需外部验证的自检测。该方法为LLM幻觉检测提供了高效实用的解决方案，Transformer探针在性能与效率上均具优势。

Abstract: Existing hallucination detection methods for large language models (LLMs) rely on external verification at inference time, requiring gold answers, retrieval systems, or auxiliary judge models. We ask whether this external supervision can instead be distilled into the model's own representations during training, enabling hallucination detection from internal activations alone at inference time.
  We introduce a weak supervision framework that combines three complementary grounding signals: substring matching, sentence embedding similarity, and an LLM as a judge verdict to label generated responses as grounded or hallucinated without human annotation. Using this framework, we construct a 15000-sample dataset from SQuAD v2 (10500 train/development samples and a separate 5000-sample test set), where each example pairs a LLaMA-2-7B generated answer with its full per-layer hidden states and structured hallucination labels.
  We then train five probing classifiers: ProbeMLP (M0), LayerWiseMLP (M1), CrossLayerTransformer (M2), HierarchicalTransformer (M3), and CrossLayerAttentionTransformerV2 (M4), directly on these hidden states, treating external grounding signals as training-time supervision only. Our central hypothesis is that hallucination detection signals can be distilled into transformer representations, enabling internal detection without any external verification at inference time.
  Results support this hypothesis. Transformer-based probes achieve the strongest discrimination, with M2 performing best on 5-fold average AUC/F1, and M3 performing best on both single-fold validation and held-out test evaluation. We also benchmark inference efficiency: probe latency ranges from 0.15 to 5.62 ms (batched) and 1.55 to 6.66 ms (single sample), while end-to-end generation plus probe throughput remains approximately 0.231 queries per second, indicating negligible practical overhead.

</details>


### [154] [SymptomWise: A Deterministic Reasoning Layer for Reliable and Efficient AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06375)
*Isaac Henry,Avery Byrne,Christopher Giza,Ron Henry,Shahram Yazdani*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对AI症状分析系统的可靠性、可解释性和幻觉问题，本研究提出SymptomWise框架，通过分离语言理解与诊断推理，结合专家知识库、确定性推理和受限LLM使用，在42例儿科神经病例测试中达到88% top-5准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI驱动的症状分析系统在可靠性、可解释性和幻觉方面面临持续挑战，端到端生成式方法在安全关键场景中缺乏可追溯性，可能产生无支持的诊断输出。

Method: 提出SymptomWise框架，将语言理解与诊断推理分离。系统结合专家策展的医学知识、确定性代码驱动推理和受限的大语言模型使用：自由文本输入首先映射到经过验证的症状表示，然后在有限假设空间内由确定性推理模块评估，生成排序的鉴别诊断；语言模型仅用于症状提取和可选的解释生成，不参与诊断推理。

Result: 在42例专家编写的具有挑战性的儿科神经病例的初步评估中，系统输出与临床医生共识有显著重叠，88%的病例中正确诊断出现在前五位鉴别诊断中。

Conclusion: 该架构提高了系统的可追溯性，减少了无根据的结论，支持模块化评估。该框架可推广至其他溯因推理领域，可作为基础模型的确定性结构化和路由层，在有限任务中提高精度并降低不必要的计算开销。

Abstract: AI-driven symptom analysis systems face persistent challenges in reliability, interpretability, and hallucination. End-to-end generative approaches often lack traceability and may produce unsupported or inconsistent diagnostic outputs in safety-critical settings. We present SymptomWise, a framework that separates language understanding from diagnostic reasoning. The system combines expert-curated medical knowledge, deterministic codex-driven inference, and constrained use of large language models. Free-text input is mapped to validated symptom representations, then evaluated by a deterministic reasoning module operating over a finite hypothesis space to produce a ranked differential diagnosis. Language models are used only for symptom extraction and optional explanation, not for diagnostic inference. This architecture improves traceability, reduces unsupported conclusions, and enables modular evaluation of system components. Preliminary evaluation on 42 expert-authored challenging pediatric neurology cases shows meaningful overlap with clinician consensus, with the correct diagnosis appearing in the top five differentials in 88% of cases. Beyond medicine, the framework generalizes to other abductive reasoning domains and may serve as a deterministic structuring and routing layer for foundation models, improving precision and potentially reducing unnecessary computational overhead in bounded tasks.

</details>


### [155] [ProofSketcher: Hybrid LLM + Lightweight Proof Checker for Reliable Math/Logic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06401)
*Kranthi Kommuru,Kunal Khanvilkar,Gaurav Parekh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型证明错误难检测与传统定理证明器使用繁琐的矛盾，本文提出混合流水线：LLM生成紧凑DSL类型化证明草图，轻量级可信内核将其展开为显式证明义务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在数学逻辑论证中虽具说服力但易含细微错误（如忽略条件、无效推理、引用不可得引理），这些错误文本层面极难发现；而Lean、Coq等交互式证明器虽通过小可信内核确保语法语义严格可靠，但需完全形式化并输入大量底层信息，代价沉重。

Method: 构建混合证明架构——利用大语言模型生成紧凑领域特定语言（DSL）的类型化证明草图，再通过轻量级可信内核将草图自动扩展为显式证明义务，实现LLM创造力与内核严谨性的结合。

Result: 提出并实现了LLM生成与内核验证协同的混合证明范式，理论上可在保证证明可靠性的同时显著降低人工形式化成本。

Conclusion: 该方法有效平衡了形式化验证的严格性与大语言模型的生成效率，为人机协作的形式化数学证明提供了实用化路径，有望促进形式化方法在实践中的应用。

Abstract: The large language models (LLMs) might produce a persuasive argument within mathematical and logical fields, although such argument often includes some minor missteps, including the entire omission of side conditions, invalid inference patterns, or appeals to a lemma that cannot be derived logically out of the context being discussed. These omissions are infamously hard to notice solely out of the text, as even the misconstrued construction still may seem mostly accurate. Conversely, interactive theorem provers like Lean and Coq have rigorous reliability by ensuring that syntactic and semantic statements only accept statements that can pass all the syntactic and semantic steps in the program which is a small trusted kernel of the language type-checks with. Despite the fact that this technique provides strong guarantees, it comes at quite a heavy price: the evidence must be completely formalized, and the evidence user or a auxiliary search program must provide an avalanche of low-level information. This paper presents a hybrid pipeline where an LLM generates a typed proof sketch in a compact DSL and a lightweight trusted kernel expands the sketch into explicit proof obligations.

</details>


### [156] [BDI-Kit Demo: A Toolkit for Programmable and Conversational Data Harmonization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06405)
*Roque Lopez,Yurong Liu,Christos Koutras,Juliana Freire*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文介绍BDI-Kit，一个用于解决数据协调瓶颈的可扩展工具包。它提供Python API供开发者编程构建处理流水线，以及AI聊天界面供领域专家通过自然语言对话进行数据协调。演示展示了通过自动化匹配、AI辅助推理和用户驱动的迭代优化来实现模式与值匹配的两种使用场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据协调因模式、值表示和领域特定约定的异质性而成为集成分析的主要瓶颈。现有方法难以同时满足开发者的编程需求和领域专家的非技术性使用需求。

Method: BDI-Kit提供两个互补接口：面向开发者的Python API用于程序化构建协调流水线，以及AI辅助聊天界面供领域专家通过自然语言对话操作。该工具包支持可扩展的模式与值匹配，并允许用户通过自动化匹配、AI辅助推理与人工精调的混合方式进行迭代式探索、验证和改进。

Result: 演示展示了两种有效场景：(i)使用Python API编程组合基本操作、检查中间输出并重用转换规则；(ii)通过自然语言与AI助手对话访问BDI-Kit功能，并根据建议迭代优化结果。两种方式均能成功实现数据协调。

Conclusion: BDI-Kit通过提供适合不同用户群体的双界面设计，有效解决了数据协调的瓶颈问题。它结合了自动化技术的效率与人类专家的专业知识，为异质性数据的集成分析提供了灵活实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Data harmonization remains a major bottleneck for integrative analysis due to heterogeneity in schemas, value representations, and domain-specific conventions. BDI-Kit provides an extensible toolkit for schema and value matching. It exposes two complementary interfaces tailored to different user needs: a Python API enabling developers to construct harmonization pipelines programmatically, and an AI-assisted chat interface allowing domain experts to harmonize data through natural language dialogue. This demonstration showcases how users interact with BDI-Kit to iteratively explore, validate, and refine schema and value matches through a combination of automated matching, AI-assisted reasoning, and user-driven refinement. We present two scenarios: (i) using the Python API to programmatically compose primitives, examine intermediate outputs, and reuse transformations; and (ii) conversing with the AI assistant in natural language to access BDI-Kit's capabilities and iteratively refine outputs based on the assistant's suggestions.

</details>


### [157] [On Emotion-Sensitive Decision Making of Small Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06562)

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 表示层情绪诱导：使用激活引导技术，基于众包验证的真实世界情绪诱发文本；2. 博弈论评估框架：构建包含合作与竞争激励、完全与不完全信息条件的标准决策模板；3. 场景实例化：利用外交游戏、星际争霸II以及多样化的现实世界角色场景；4. 实验设计：在多种模型架构和模态上进行跨模型家族测试。

Result: 1. 情绪扰动系统性地影响了模型的战略选择；2. 然而，由此产生的不稳定行为与人类期望不完全一致；3. 不同模型家族表现出不同的敏感性模式。

Abstract: Small language models (SLM) are increasingly used as interactive decision-making agents, yet most decision-oriented evaluations ignore emotion as a causal factor influencing behavior. We study emotion-sensitive decision making by combining representation-level emotion induction with a structured game-theoretic evaluation. Emotional states are induced using activation steering derived from crowd-validated, real-world emotion-eliciting texts, enabling controlled and transferable interventions beyond prompt-based methods. We introduce a benchmark built around canonical decision templates that span cooperative and competitive incentives under both complete and incomplete information. These templates are instantiated using strategic scenarios from \textsc{Diplomacy}, \textsc{StarCraft II}, and diverse real-world personas. Experiments across multiple model families in various architecture and modalities, show that emotional perturbations systematically affect strategic choices, but the resulting behaviors are often unstable and not fully aligned with human expectations. Finally, we outline an approach to improve robustness to emotion-driven perturbations.

### [158] [Rethinking Generalization in Reasoning SFT: A Conditional Analysis on Optimization, Data, and Model Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06628)
*Qihan Ren,Peng Wang,Ruikun Cai,Shuai Shao,Dadi Guo,Yuejin Xie,Yafu Li,Quanshi Zhang,Xia Hu,Jing Shao,Dongrui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了"监督微调仅记忆、强化学习才泛化"的主流观点，发现长链式思维监督下的推理SFT具备条件性泛化能力，其表现受优化动态、数据质量和基座模型能力共同影响，且存在推理提升与安全退化的不对称现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视监督微调(SFT)与强化学习(RL)在泛化能力上的传统认知，针对长思维链(CoT)监督的推理任务，探究SFT是否真的缺乏跨领域泛化能力。

Method: 通过系统分析优化动力学、训练数据特性与基座模型能力三因素对跨领域泛化的影响，识别训练不足导致的"下降-恢复"模式，并对比不同数据质量和模型强度下的泛化表现。

Result: 1) 泛化非缺失而是条件性：性能随训练呈现先降后升的"下降-恢复"模式；2) 数据质量决定泛化效果：验证后的长CoT轨迹带来持续增益；3) 模型能力至关重要：强模型内化可迁移过程模式，弱模型仅模仿表层表达；4) 泛化不对称：推理能力提升伴随安全性退化。

Conclusion: 应将问题从"推理SFT能否泛化"转向"在何种条件下以何种代价泛化"，强调优化充分性、数据质量和模型能力是可控条件，而安全-推理权衡是不可忽视的成本。

Abstract: A prevailing narrative in LLM post-training holds that supervised finetuning (SFT) memorizes while reinforcement learning (RL) generalizes. We revisit this claim for reasoning SFT with long chain-of-thought (CoT) supervision and find that cross-domain generalization is not absent but conditional, jointly shaped by optimization dynamics, training data, and base-model capability. Some reported failures are under-optimization artifacts: cross-domain performance first degrades before recovering and improving with extended training (a dip-and-recovery pattern), so shorttraining checkpoints can underestimate generalization. Data quality and structure both matter: low-quality solutions broadly hurt generalization,while verified long-CoT traces yield consistent cross-domain gains. Model capability is essential: stronger models internalize transferable procedural patterns (e.g., backtracking) even from a toy arithmetic game, while weaker ones imitate surface verbosity. This generalization is asymmetric, however: reasoning improves while safety degrades, reframing the question from whether reasoning SFT generalizes to under what conditions and at what cost.

### [159] [ATANT: An Evaluation Framework for AI Continuity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06710)
*Samuel Sameer Tanguturi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ATANT评估框架，通过250个故事和1835个验证问题的叙事语料库，系统性地衡量AI系统的连续性能力，参考实现准确率从58%提升至96%，解决了现有记忆组件缺乏标准化评估的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI行业虽已开发RAG管道、向量数据库等多种记忆组件，但缺乏公开框架来正式定义和测量这些组件是否产生真正的连续性。连续性是系统持久化、更新、消歧和重建上下文的关键能力，现有技术无法有效评估这一属性。

Method: 研究定义了包含7个必要属性的连续性系统特性，提出10个检查点的评估方法（无需LLM参与评估循环），并构建包含6个生活领域、250个故事和1835个验证问题的叙事测试语料库，通过5轮迭代从隔离模式到累积模式进行系统验证。

Result: 参考实现从遗留架构的58%准确率逐步提升至隔离模式250个故事下的100%，50个故事累积模式下的100%，以及250个故事累积规模下的96%。累积模式是核心测试指标，要求系统在250个并存叙事中准确检索事实且无交叉污染。

Conclusion: ATANT作为系统无关、模型独立的序列化方法论，为构建和验证连续性系统提供了标准化工具。框架已开源，完整语料库将逐步发布，填补了AI连续性评估的空白，对推动记忆系统发展具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present ATANT (Automated Test for Acceptance of Narrative Truth), an open evaluation framework for measuring continuity in AI systems: the ability to persist, update, disambiguate, and reconstruct meaningful context across time. While the AI industry has produced memory components (RAG pipelines, vector databases, long context windows, profile layers), no published framework formally defines or measures whether these components produce genuine continuity. We define continuity as a system property with 7 required properties, introduce a 10-checkpoint evaluation methodology that operates without an LLM in the evaluation loop, and present a narrative test corpus of 250 stories comprising 1,835 verification questions across 6 life domains. We evaluate a reference implementation across 5 test suite iterations, progressing from 58% (legacy architecture) to 100% in isolated mode (250 stories) and 100% in 50-story cumulative mode, with 96% at 250-story cumulative scale. The cumulative result is the primary measure: when 250 distinct life narratives coexist in the same database, the system must retrieve the correct fact for the correct context without cross-contamination. ATANT is system-agnostic, model-independent, and designed as a sequenced methodology for building and validating continuity systems. The framework specification, example stories, and evaluation protocol are available at https://github.com/Kenotic-Labs/ATANT. The full 250-story corpus will be released incrementally.

### [160] [Reasoning Fails Where Step Flow Breaks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06695)
*Xiaoyu Xu,Yulan Pan,Xiaosong Yuan,Zhihong Shen,Minghao Su,Yuanhao Su,Xiaofeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对大型推理模型行为不稳定且难以解释的问题，提出Step-Saliency方法分析信息流，揭示浅层锁定与深层衰减两种失败模式，并设计StepFlow测试时干预策略，在不重新训练的情况下提升多领域任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型虽在数学、科学和代码等复杂任务上表现优异，但其长链式推理行为仍不稳定且难以解释，现有分析工具难以有效处理长结构化推理轨迹，亟需新的分析框架和改进方法来理解和提升模型推理能力。

Method: 提出Step-Saliency方法，沿问题-思考-摘要轨迹将注意力-梯度分数池化为步骤到步骤的显著性映射；并基于此设计StepFlow测试时干预，通过奇偶均衡桥接(Odds-Equal Bridge)调整浅层显著性模式，通过步骤动量注入(Step Momentum Injection)在深层添加步骤级残差连接。

Result: StepFlow在无需重新训练的前提下，显著提升了多个大型推理模型在数学、科学和代码任务上的准确率，验证了修复信息流能够有效恢复模型部分缺失的推理性能。

Conclusion: 研究证实，通过针对性修复推理过程中的信息流动缺陷，可以显著提升大型推理模型的推理性能，这为模型优化提供了新的理论视角和实践路径。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) that generate long chains of thought now perform well on multi-step math, science, and coding tasks. However, their behavior is still unstable and hard to interpret, and existing analysis tools struggle with such long, structured reasoning traces. We introduce Step-Saliency, which pools attention--gradient scores into step-to-step maps along the question--thinking--summary trajectory. Across several models, Step-Saliency reveals two recurring information-flow failures: Shallow Lock-in, where shallow layers over-focus on the current step and barely use earlier context, and Deep Decay, where deep layers gradually lose saliency on the thinking segment and the summary increasingly attends to itself and the last few steps. Motivated by these patterns, we propose StepFlow, a saliency-inspired test-time intervention that adjusts shallow saliency patterns measured by Step-Saliency via Odds-Equal Bridge and adds a small step-level residual in deep layers via Step Momentum Injection. StepFlow improves accuracy on math, science, and coding tasks across multiple LRMs without retraining, indicating that repairing information flow can recover part of their missing reasoning performance.

### [161] [AgentGate: A Lightweight Structured Routing Engine for the Internet of Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06696)
*Yujun Cheng,Enfang Cui,Hao Qin,Zhiyuan Liang,Qi Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对AI智能体在互联网环境下的高效调度问题，本文提出AgentGate——一种轻量级结构化路由引擎。该方法将路由重构为两阶段约束决策问题（行动决策+结构实例化），并通过候选感知微调使3B-7B紧凑模型在资源受限条件下实现竞争性性能，为隐私敏感场景提供可行解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI智能体系统在本地设备、边缘节点、私有服务和云平台间的快速发展，请求调度面临延迟、隐私和成本等多重约束挑战。尽管智能体命名、发现和交互有所改进，但现有方法将路由视为无约束文本生成，难以满足实际系统要求。

Method: 提出AgentGate框架，核心创新包括：1）将路由建模为约束决策问题而非自由文本生成；2）两阶段分解：行动决策阶段（判断单智能体调用、多智能体规划、直接响应或安全升级）和结构grounding阶段（将行动实例化为可执行输出）；3）设计路由导向微调方案，采用候选感知监督和困难负样本训练策略。

Result: 在自建路由基准测试中，参数量为3B-7B的开源紧凑模型展现出具有竞争力的路由性能。不同模型间的性能差异主要体现在三个维度：行动预测准确率、候选智能体选择质量以及结构化grounding的精确度。

Conclusion: 研究表明结构化路由是构建高效隐私感知智能体系统的可行设计范式，特别适合资源受限的部署环境。该工作为智能体互联网中的请求分发问题提供了新思路。

Abstract: The rapid development of AI agent systems is leading to an emerging Internet of Agents, where specialized agents operate across local devices, edge nodes, private services, and cloud platforms. Although recent efforts have improved agent naming, discovery, and interaction, efficient request dispatch remains an open systems problem under latency, privacy, and cost constraints. In this paper, we present AgentGate, a lightweight structured routing engine for candidate-aware agent dispatch. Instead of treating routing as unrestricted text generation, AgentGate formulates it as a constrained decision problem and decomposes it into two stages: action decision and structural grounding. The first stage determines whether a query should trigger single-agent invocation, multi-agent planning, direct response, or safe escalation, while the second stage instantiates the selected action into executable outputs such as target agents, structured arguments, or multi-step plans. To adapt compact models to this setting, we further develop a routing-oriented fine-tuning scheme with candidate-aware supervision and hard negative examples. Experiments on a curated routing benchmark with several 3B--7B open-weight models show that compact models can provide competitive routing performance in constrained settings, and that model differences are mainly reflected in action prediction, candidate selection, and structured grounding quality. These results indicate that structured routing is a feasible design point for efficient and privacy-aware agent systems, especially when routing decisions must be made under resource-constrained deployment conditions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从4470份人类对AI幻觉的响应数据出发，按人类验证难度将幻觉划分为显性与隐性两类；进而提出激活空间干预方法，分别为两类幻觉学习独立探针，实现对模型验证性的差异化调控。

Result: 实证结果表明该方法有效，针对性干预在调节对应验证性方面性能优越；通过简单混合两类干预，即可灵活适配不同场景的验证性需求。

Abstract: AI applications driven by multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are prone to hallucinations and pose considerable risks to human users. Crucially, such hallucinations are not equally problematic: some hallucination contents could be detected by human users(i.e., obvious hallucinations), while others are often missed or require more verification effort(i.e., elusive hallucinations). This indicates that multimodal AI hallucinations vary significantly in their verifiability. Yet, little research has explored how to control this property for AI applications with diverse security and usability demands. To address this gap, we construct a dataset from 4,470 human responses to AI-generated hallucinations and categorize these hallucinations into obvious and elusive types based on their verifiability by human users. Further, we propose an activation-space intervention method that learns separate probes for obvious and elusive hallucinations. We reveal that obvious and elusive hallucinations elicit different intervention probes, allowing for fine-grained control over the model's verifiability. Empirical results demonstrate the efficacy of this approach and show that targeted interventions yield superior performance in regulating corresponding verifiability. Moreover, simply mixing these interventions enables flexible control over the verifiability required for different scenarios.

### [163] [TurboAgent: An LLM-Driven Autonomous Multi-Agent Framework for Turbomachinery Aerodynamic Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06747)
*Juan Du,Yueteng Wu,Pan Zhao,Yuze Liu,Min Zhang,Xiaobin Xu,Xinglong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出TurboAgent，一种基于大语言模型的多智能体自主框架，用于涡轮机械气动设计与优化。该框架通过LLM协调专用智能体完成生成式设计、性能预测、多目标优化和物理验证，实现了从自然语言需求到最终设计的端到端闭环。在跨音速单级压气机验证中，30分钟内完成设计，性能指标R²>0.91，优化后效率提升1.61%、压比提升3.02%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能设计方法通常聚焦于单个设计阶段或依赖松耦合流水线，难以实现完全自主的端到端设计。传统试错式设计效率低下，且涡轮机械设计各阶段耦合紧密，亟需一种集成化框架来协同处理几何生成、性能预测、优化和验证等全流程任务。

Method: TurboAgent采用大语言模型作为核心协调器，负责任务规划和智能体管理。系统包含四个专用智能体：生成式设计智能体、快速性能预测智能体、多目标优化智能体和基于物理的验证智能体。该框架将传统试错流程转变为数据驱动的协同工作流，保留高保真CFD模拟用于最终验证。

Result: 在跨音速单级压气机验证中，目标性能、生成设计与CFD模拟之间表现出强一致性：质量流量、总压比和等熵效率的判定系数(R²)均超过0.91，归一化均方根误差低于8%。优化智能体进一步将等熵效率提升1.61%，总压比提升3.02%。在并行计算条件下，完整工作流可在约30分钟内完成。

Conclusion: TurboAgent成功实现了从自然语言需求到最终设计生成的自主闭环设计流程，为涡轮机械气动设计提供了高效、可扩展的新范式，显著提升了设计自动化水平和效率。

Abstract: The aerodynamic design of turbomachinery is a complex and tightly coupled multi-stage process involving geometry generation, performance prediction, optimization, and high-fidelity physical validation. Existing intelligent design approaches typically focus on individual stages or rely on loosely coupled pipelines, making fully autonomous end-to-end design challenging.To address this issue, this study proposes TurboAgent, a large language model (LLM)-driven autonomous multi-agent framework for turbomachinery aerodynamic design and optimization. The LLM serves as the core for task planning and coordination, while specialized agents handle generative design, rapid performance prediction, multi-objective optimization, and physics-based validation. The framework transforms traditional trial-and-error design into a data-driven collaborative workflow, with high-fidelity simulations retained for final verification.A transonic single-rotor compressor is used for validation. The results show strong agreement between target performance, generated designs, and CFD simulations. The coefficients of determination (R2) for mass flow rate, total pressure ratio, and isentropic efficiency all exceed 0.91, with normalized RMSE values below 8%. The optimization agent further improves isentropic efficiency by 1.61% and total pressure ratio by 3.02%. The complete workflow can be executed within approximately 30 minutes under parallel computing.
  These results demonstrate that TurboAgent enables an autonomous closed-loop design process from natural language requirements to final design generation, providing an efficient and scalable paradigm for turbomachinery aerodynamic design

</details>


### [164] [Riemann-Bench: A Benchmark for Moonshot Mathematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06802)

TL;DR: 该论文指出AI虽已具备IMO金牌水平的竞赛数学能力，但竞赛数学仅体现狭窄的数学推理范畴。为此提出\b bench{}基准，包含25个由顶尖数学专家设计的研究级难题，每个问题作者独立求解需耗时数周。通过双盲验证和程序化验证器评估前沿模型，结果显示所有模型得分均低于10%，揭示了AI在真正研究级数学推理能力上的巨大鸿沟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI系统虽在国际数学奥林匹克竞赛(IMO)中达到金牌水平，但竞赛数学仅涵盖有限领域、依赖技巧而非深层理论，无法代表真正的数学研究能力。因此需要构建一个能评估AI在超出竞赛边界的研究级数学问题上表现的新基准，以检验其是否具备深度理论知识和创造性推理能力。

Method: 1) 构建\b bench{}：收录25个由常春藤联盟数学教授、研究生及IMO金牌得主设计的研究级难题，每道题作者独立求解耗时数周；2) 质量控制：采用双盲验证机制，由两名独立领域专家从零开始求解验证；3) 评估方式：每道题有唯一闭式解，通过程序化验证器自动评判；4) 模型测试：将前沿模型作为无约束研究智能体，提供完整编码工具、搜索能力和开放式推理环境；5) 统计方法：每道题进行100次独立运行计算无偏统计估计量。

Result: 在所有前沿模型的测试中，得分均低于10%，表明当前AI系统在研究级数学推理能力上与人类专家存在巨大差距。这一结果量化了竞赛级问题求解能力与真正研究级数学能力之间的鸿沟。

Conclusion: AI系统在竞赛数学上的成功并不能转化为研究级数学推理能力。通过保持基准完全私有化，确保了测量性能反映的是真实数学能力而非训练数据记忆。该研究揭示了当前AI在深度数学理论理解和创新性证明构造方面的根本性不足，为未来研究方向提供了重要基准。

Abstract: Recent AI systems have achieved gold-medal-level performance on the International Mathematical Olympiad, demonstrating remarkable proficiency at competition-style problem solving. However, competition mathematics represents only a narrow slice of mathematical reasoning: problems are drawn from limited domains, require minimal advanced machinery, and can often reward insightful tricks over deep theoretical knowledge. We introduce \bench{}, a private benchmark of 25 expert-curated problems designed to evaluate AI systems on research-level mathematics that goes far beyond the olympiad frontier. Problems are authored by Ivy League mathematics professors, graduate students, and PhD-holding IMO medalists, and routinely took their authors weeks to solve independently. Each problem undergoes double-blind verification by two independent domain experts who must solve the problem from scratch, and yields a unique, closed-form solution assessed by programmatic verifiers. We evaluate frontier models as unconstrained research agents, with full access to coding tools, search, and open-ended reasoning, using an unbiased statistical estimator computed over 100 independent runs per problem. Our results reveal that all frontier models currently score below 10\%, exposing a substantial gap between olympiad-level problem solving and genuine research-level mathematical reasoning. By keeping the benchmark fully private, we ensure that measured performance reflects authentic mathematical capability rather than memorization of training data.

Method: 创新性地提出UILoop范式，将GUI推理任务视为循环式的屏幕-UI元素-动作过程，通过让MLLMs显式学习关键UI元素的定位、语义功能和实际应用，实现精准元素发现与可解释推理。

### [166] [CAFP: A Post-Processing Framework for Group Fairness via Counterfactual Model Averaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07009)
*Irina Arévalo,Marcos Oliva*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出CAFP（反事实平均公平预测），一种模型无关的后处理方法，通过翻转敏感属性生成反事实样本并平均预测结果，无需重新训练即可消除模型对受保护属性的依赖，在理论上保证人口统计均等性并显著降低机会均等差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习在信贷、医疗、刑事司法等敏感领域的部署面临公平性挑战。现有预处理方法需要完全控制模型架构和敏感属性信息，在实际系统中往往不可行。需要开发一种无需修改原始分类器或重新训练的后处理方案。

Method: Counterfactual Averaging for Fair Predictions (CAFP) - 对每个输入生成敏感属性翻转的反事实版本，将原始模型在事实样本和反事实样本上的预测结果进行平均，从而消除敏感属性的不公平影响。该方法具有模型无关性，属于后处理技术。

Result: 理论分析表明：1) 消除预测对受保护属性的直接依赖；2) 降低预测与敏感属性间的互信息；3) 相对于原始模型的失真度可证明有界；4) 在温和假设下可实现完美的人口统计均等性；5) 将机会均等差距至少降低一半的平均反事实偏差。

Conclusion: CAFP提供了一种实用且理论完备的公平性干预方案，特别适用于无法访问模型内部或敏感属性的实际场景，为敏感领域的公平预测提供了新思路。

Abstract: Ensuring fairness in machine learning predictions is a critical challenge, especially when models are deployed in sensitive domains such as credit scoring, healthcare, and criminal justice. While many fairness interventions rely on data preprocessing or algorithmic constraints during training, these approaches often require full control over the model architecture and access to protected attribute information, which may not be feasible in real-world systems. In this paper, we propose Counterfactual Averaging for Fair Predictions (CAFP), a model-agnostic post-processing method that mitigates unfair influence from protected attributes without retraining or modifying the original classifier. CAFP operates by generating counterfactual versions of each input in which the sensitive attribute is flipped, and then averaging the model's predictions across factual and counterfactual instances. We provide a theoretical analysis of CAFP, showing that it eliminates direct dependence on the protected attribute, reduces mutual information between predictions and sensitive attributes, and provably bounds the distortion introduced relative to the original model. Under mild assumptions, we further show that CAFP achieves perfect demographic parity and reduces the equalized odds gap by at least half the average counterfactual bias.

As a result, current resources provide limited support for testing whether a model can use remembered interaction history to interpret a user's present affective state.
  We introduce A-MBER, an Affective Memory Benchmark for Emotion Recognition, to evaluate this capability. A-MBER focuses on present affective interpretation grounded in remembered multi-session interaction history. Given an interaction trajectory and a designated anchor turn, a model must infer the user's current affective state, identify historically relevant evidence, and justify its interpretation in a grounded way. The benchmark is constructed through a staged pipeline with explicit intermediate representations, including long-horizon planning, conversation generation, annotation, question construction, and final packaging. It supports judgment, retrieval, and explanation tasks, together with robustness settings such as modality degradation and insufficient-evidence conditions.
  Experiments compare local-context, long-context, retrieved-memory, structured-memory, and gold-evidence conditions within a unified framework. Results show that A-MBER is especially discriminative on the subsets it is designed to stress, including long-range implicit affect, high-dependency memory levels, trajectory-based reasoning, and adversarial settings. ### [168] [Planning Task Shielding: Detecting and Repairing Flaws in Planning Tasks through Turning them Unsolvable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07042)
*Alberto Pozanco,Marianela Morales,Pietro Totis,Daniel Borrajo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出规划任务屏蔽问题，通过检测并修复规划任务中的缺陷状态，使包含缺陷状态的任务变得不可解。核心贡献是$allmin$最优算法，该算法通过最小化修改原始动作来实现任务不可解，从而确保缺陷状态不可达。实验验证了该算法在不同规模任务上的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出$allmin$最优算法，通过寻找对原始动作的最小修改集合，使规划任务变得不可解，从而实现规划任务屏蔽。该方法直接修改任务定义而非运行时监控，确保任何计划都无法到达缺陷状态。

Result: 在规模递增的规划任务上进行实证评估表明，$allmin$能够有效屏蔽系统缺陷，通过使规划任务不可解的方式确保缺陷状态不被达到，验证了算法的实用性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: 规划任务屏蔽为规划缺陷的静态修复提供了新范式，$allmin$作为最优算法，通过最小修改实现任务不可解，为构建安全可靠的规划系统提供了理论基础和实践工具。

Abstract: Most research in planning focuses on generating a plan to achieve a desired set of goals. However, a goal specification can also be used to encode a property that should never hold, allowing a planner to identify a trace that would reach a flawed state. In such cases, the objective may shift to modifying the planning task to ensure that the flawed state is never reached-in other words, to make the planning task unsolvable. In this paper we introduce planning task shielding: the problem of detecting and repairing flaws in planning tasks. We propose $allmin$, an optimal algorithm that solves these tasks by minimally modifying the original actions to render the planning task unsolvable. We empirically evaluate the performance of $allmin$ in shielding planning tasks of increasing size, showing how it can effectively shield the system by turning the planning task unsolvable.

### [170] [Reason in Chains, Learn in Trees: Self-Rectification and Grafting for Multi-turn Agent Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07165)
*Yu Li,Sizhe Tang,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出T-STAR框架，通过构建认知树挖掘独立轨迹间的潜在关联结构，采用回溯估值机制实现步骤级优势估计，结合思维嫁接与外科手术式策略优化，显著提升LLM智能体在稀疏奖励的多步推理任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（如GRPO）将采样轨迹视为独立链，对所有步骤均匀赋分，忽略了关键步骤对推理结果的过度影响，导致多步推理任务中稀疏奖励问题制约了LLM智能体的强化学习效果。

Method: 1）认知树构建：识别并合并功能相似的步骤/节点，整合多轨迹为统一树结构；2）内省式估值：通过树结构回溯传播轨迹级奖励，获得方差缩减的步骤级相对优势；3）上下文思维嫁接：在关键分歧点对比成败分支，合成修正性推理；4）外科手术式策略优化：利用Bradley-Terry损失函数聚焦关键步骤的丰富策略梯度信息。

Result: 在具身交互、推理规划等多类基准测试中实现持续性能提升，尤其在需要扩展推理链的任务上增益最显著。

Conclusion: T-STAR通过显式建模轨迹间关联并聚焦关键推理步骤，有效缓解了稀疏奖励问题，为提升LLM智能体的复杂推理能力提供了新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning for Large Language Model agents is often hindered by sparse rewards in multi-step reasoning tasks. Existing approaches like Group Relative Policy Optimization treat sampled trajectories as independent chains, assigning uniform credit to all steps in each chain and ignoring the existence of critical steps that may disproportionally impact reasoning outcome. In this paper, we propose T-STAR(Tree-structured Self-Taught Agent Rectification), a framework that recovers the latent correlated reward structure across seemingly independent trajectories. Specifically, we consolidate trajectories into a unified Cognitive Tree by identifying and merging functionally similar steps/nodes. It enables an Introspective Valuation mechanism that back-propagates trajectory-level rewards through the tree to obtain a new notion of variance-reduced relative advantage at step-level. Using the Cognitive Tree, we also develop In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches at critical divergence points/steps. Our proposed Surgical Policy Optimization then capitalizes on the rich policy gradient information concentrated at these critical points/steps through a Bradley-Terry type of surgical loss. Extensive experiments across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks demonstrate that T-STAR achieves consistent improvements over strong baselines, with gains most pronounced on tasks requiring extended reasoning chains.

### [171] [How Much LLM Does a Self-Revising Agent Actually Need?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07236)
*Seongwoo Jeong,Seonil Son*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出声明式反射运行时协议，将大型语言模型智能体的内部状态、置信度信号、保护动作及假设转移外部化为可观测的运行时结构。通过在协作战舰游戏上的实验，研究将智能体能力分解为后验信念追踪、显式世界模型规划、符号化片段反思和稀疏LLM修订四个组件，发现显式规划显著优于基线（胜率+24.1pp，F1+0.017），而稀疏LLM修订仅带来微小且非单调的改进，主要贡献在于使LLM的边际作用可直接研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大型语言模型的智能体常将世界建模、规划与反思整合于单一模型循环中，导致无法科学区分能力来源：究竟来自模型本身还是外围结构。本文旨在通过经验化方法使这一问题可处理，从而揭示LLM在智能体中的实际作用。

Method: 作者设计声明式反射运行时协议，将智能体状态、置信信号、保护动作与假设转移外部化为可检查结构。在声明式运行时中实现该协议，并在含噪声的协作战舰游戏上评估四种逐步结构化的智能体，实验涵盖54局游戏（18个棋盘×3个随机种子）。

Result: 实验分解出四个核心组件：后验信念追踪、显式世界模型规划、符号化片段内反思与稀疏LLM修订。显式世界模型规划相较贪婪后验跟随基线显著提升性能（胜率+24.1个百分点，F1+0.017）。符号化反思作为真实运行时机制有效运行。在约4.3%的回合添加条件性LLM修订仅产生微小非单调变化：F1平均上升0.005，但胜率下降（54局中从31胜降至29胜）。

Conclusion: 本研究的核心贡献在于方法论层面：通过外部化反思机制，将原本潜在的智能体行为转化为可观测的运行时结构，从而能够直接量化分析LLM干预的边际作用，而非追求性能排行榜上的突破。

Abstract: Recent LLM-based agents often place world modeling, planning, and reflection inside a single language model loop. This can produce capable behavior, but it makes a basic scientific question difficult to answer: which part of the agent's competence actually comes from the LLM, and which part comes from explicit structure around it?
  We study this question not by claiming a general answer, but by making it empirically tractable. We introduce a declared reflective runtime protocol that externalizes agent state, confidence signals, guarded actions, and hypothetical transitions into inspectable runtime structure. We instantiate this protocol in a declarative runtime and evaluate it on noisy Collaborative Battleship [4] using four progressively structured agents over 54 games (18 boards $\times$ 3 seeds).
  The resulting decomposition isolates four components: posterior belief tracking, explicit world-model planning, symbolic in-episode reflection, and sparse LLM-based revision. Across this decomposition, explicit world-model planning improves substantially over a greedy posterior-following baseline (+24.1pp win rate, +0.017 F1). Symbolic reflection operates as a real runtime mechanism -- with prediction tracking, confidence gating, and guarded revision actions -- even though its current revision presets are not yet net-positive in aggregate. Adding conditional LLM revision at about 4.3\% of turns yields only a small and non-monotonic change: average F1 rises slightly (+0.005) while win rate drops (31$\rightarrow$29 out of 54).
  These results suggest a methodological contribution rather than a leaderboard claim: externalizing reflection turns otherwise latent agent behavior into inspectable runtime structure, allowing the marginal role of LLM intervention to be studied directly.

</details>

### [172] [EviSnap: Faithful Evidence-Cited Explanations for Cold-Start Cross-Domain Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06172)
*Yingjun Dai,Ahmed El-Roby*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对跨域推荐冷启动问题，现有方法存在解释不透明或难以审计的缺陷。本文提出EviSnap轻量级框架，通过LLM离线蒸馏评论为带原文证据的方面卡片，构建领域无关概念库，并采用线性概念映射实现可解释且忠实的预测。在Amazon数据集六个迁移任务上超越基线并通过忠实性测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有冷启动跨域推荐系统或采用不透明嵌入映射，或依赖LLM生成的后期解释，这些方法缺乏可验证性和可审计性，限制了模型的可信度和可调试性。

Method: EviSnap首先利用LLM将噪声评论蒸馏为紧凑方面卡片，每个方面配verbatim支持句；然后聚类方面嵌入构建共享领域无关概念库；接着通过证据加权池化计算用户正向、用户负向和物品存在激活；再通过单一线性概念映射实现跨域迁移；最后线性评分头产生可加性贡献，支持精确分解和基于证据的反事实编辑。

Result: 在Amazon Reviews数据集的Books、Movies、Music三领域间六个迁移任务上，EviSnap持续优于强基线，并通过了删除和充分性解释忠实性测试。

Conclusion: EviSnap通过"解释即构建"设计，提供了轻量级、可审计的跨域推荐方案，在性能和解释忠实性上均表现优异，为可解释推荐开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Cold-start cross-domain recommender (CDR) systems predict a user's preferences in a target domain using only their source-domain behavior, yet existing CDR models either map opaque embeddings or rely on post-hoc or LLM-generated rationales that are hard to audit. We introduce EviSnap a lightweight CDR framework whose predictions are explained by construction with evidence-cited, faithful rationales. EviSnap distills noisy reviews into compact facet cards using an LLM offline, pairing each facet with verbatim supporting sentences. It then induces a shared, domain-agnostic concept bank by clustering facet embeddings and computes user-positive, user-negative, and item-presence concept activations via evidence-weighted pooling. A single linear concept-to-concept map transfers users across domains, and a linear scoring head yields per-concept additive contributions, enabling exact score decompositions and counterfactual 'what-if' edits grounded in the cited sentences. Experiments on the Amazon Reviews dataset across six transfers among Books, Movies, and Music show that EviSnap consistently outperforms strong mapping and review-text baselines while passing deletion- and sufficiency-based tests for explanation faithfulness.

</details>


### [173] [Beyond Case Law: Evaluating Structure-Aware Retrieval and Safety in Statute-Centric Legal QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06173)
*Kyubyung Chae,Jewon Yeom,Jeongjae Park,Seunghyun Bae,Ijun Jang,Hyunbin Jin,Jinkwan Jang,Taesup Kim*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: SearchFireSafety是一个面向法规中心法律问答的结构化与安全感知基准测试，以消防安全法规为实例，评估模型检索分层碎片化证据及在不充分上下文下安全拒绝回答的能力。研究发现图引导检索显著提升性能，但揭示了关键安全权衡：领域适配模型在关键证据缺失时更易产生幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有法律问答基准主要聚焦于判例法，忽视了法规中心监管推理的独特挑战。在法规领域，相关证据分布于分层关联文档中，形成法规检索鸿沟，导致传统检索器失效，模型在上下文不完整时易产生幻觉。

Method: 提出SearchFireSafety基准，采用双源评估框架：结合需要引用感知检索的真实世界问题与合成部分上下文场景，压力测试模型的幻觉和拒绝行为。该基准在消防安全法规上实例化，专门评估模型对分层碎片化证据的检索能力及安全 abstention 机制。

Result: 多模型实验表明，图引导检索大幅提升性能；但存在关键安全权衡：领域适配模型在关键法规证据缺失时，产生幻觉的概率显著增加。

Conclusion: 研究强调需要能够联合评估法规中心监管场景中分层检索与模型安全的基准测试，以推动更可靠的法律AI系统发展。

Abstract: Legal QA benchmarks have predominantly focused on case law, overlooking the unique challenges of statute-centric regulatory reasoning. In statutory domains, relevant evidence is distributed across hierarchically linked documents, creating a statutory retrieval gap where conventional retrievers fail and models often hallucinate under incomplete context. We introduce SearchFireSafety, a structure- and safety-aware benchmark for statute-centric legal QA. Instantiated on fire-safety regulations as a representative case, the benchmark evaluates whether models can retrieve hierarchically fragmented evidence and safely abstain when statutory context is insufficient. SearchFireSafety adopts a dual-source evaluation framework combining real-world questions that require citation-aware retrieval and synthetic partial-context scenarios that stress-test hallucination and refusal behavior. Experiments across multiple large language models show that graph-guided retrieval substantially improves performance, but also reveal a critical safety trade-off: domain-adapted models are more likely to hallucinate when key statutory evidence is missing. Our findings highlight the need for benchmarks that jointly evaluate hierarchical retrieval and model safety in statute-centric regulatory settings.

### [174] [Robustness Risk of Conversational Retrieval: Identifying and Mitigating Noise Sensitivity in Qwen3-Embedding Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06176)
*Weishu Chen,Zhouhui Hou,Mingjie Zhan,Zhicheng Zhao,Fei Su*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 研究发现在真实对话检索场景中，Qwen3嵌入模型存在健壮性缺陷：结构化的对话噪声即使缺乏语义信息也会过度出现在高排名结果中，而轻量级查询提示能有效缓解该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话检索研究缺乏对真实部署环境的考量，实际应用中查询往往简短、对话化且表述模糊，检索语料包含结构化对话工件。标准基准测试无法揭示此类健壮性漏洞，需要探索模型在真实场景下的表现。

Method: 通过实证研究聚焦Qwen3嵌入模型，在不同模型规模上测试对话检索表现，与早期Qwen变体及主流密集检索基线进行对比，并系统评估轻量级查询提示对噪声入侵的抑制效果。

Result: 发现Qwen3存在部署相关的健壮性漏洞：结构化对话噪声过度可检索并侵入排名前列，该现象跨模型规模一致存在，在标准干净查询基准中难以察觉，且较早期Qwen变体及其他基线更为显著。轻量级查询提示能定性改变检索行为，有效抑制噪声入侵并恢复排名稳定性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了对话检索领域一个尚未充分探索的健壮性风险，强调评估协议必须反映部署系统的复杂性，同时表明轻量级查询提示是应对该风险的实用有效方案。

Abstract: We present an empirical study of embedding-based retrieval under realistic conversational settings, where queries are short, dialogue-like, and weakly specified, and retrieval corpora contain structured conversational artifacts. Focusing on Qwen3-embedding models, we identify a deployment-relevant robustness vulnerability: under conversational retrieval without query prompting, structured dialogue-style noise can become disproportionately retrievable and intrude into top-ranked results, despite being semantically uninformative. This failure mode emerges consistently across model scales, remains largely invisible under standard clean-query benchmarks, and is significantly more pronounced in Qwen3 than in earlier Qwen variants and other widely used dense retrieval baselines. We further show that lightweight query prompting qualitatively alters retrieval behavior, effectively suppressing noise intrusion and restoring ranking stability. Our findings highlight an underexplored robustness risk in conversational retrieval and underscore the importance of evaluation protocols that reflect the complexities of deployed systems.

</details>


### [175] [WebExpert: domain-aware web agents with critic-guided expert experience for high-precision search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06177)
*Yuelin Hu,Zhengxue Cheng,Ronghua Wu,Qunshan Gu,Hongwei Hu,Wei Liu,Qiao Liang,Li Song*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: WebExpert是一个面向金融、生物医学和医药领域的领域感知网页智能体，通过句子级经验检索与主题合并、基于弱监督的轻量级分面归纳以及偏好优化的规划，在GAIA、GPQA、HLE和WebWalkerQA数据集上比最强基线提升1.5-3.6个百分点的精确匹配率，同时减少页面跳转次数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融、生物医学和医药等专业领域的网页任务面临查询漂移、证据噪声大和推理脆弱等挑战，主要原因是缺乏领域先验知识。传统方法依赖静态手工词典，难以适应动态变化的领域需求。

Method: 提出WebExpert框架，包含三个核心组件：(i) 句子级经验检索结合主题合并与规则蒸馏；(ii) 轻量级分面归纳，通过弱监督自动构建时间、地区、政策和行业等动态分面，替代静态词典；(iii) 偏好优化的规划，通过成对偏好学习和覆盖感知目标联合优化查询规划与检索。推理时使用轻量级经验门控机制，在低检索置信度时启用回退策略。

Result: 在GAIA、GPQA、HLE和WebWalkerQA四个基准测试中，WebExpert相比最强浏览基线将答案精确匹配率提升1.5-3.6个百分点，并有效减少了页面跳转次数。消融实验验证了检索、主题合并、分面归纳和偏好感知训练各模块的贡献。

Conclusion: WebExpert通过动态领域知识获取和偏好优化机制，显著提升了专业领域网页任务的准确性和效率，证明了端到端领域感知架构的有效性。

Abstract: Specialized web tasks in finance, biomedicine, and pharmaceuticals remain challenging due to missing domain priors: queries drift, evidence is noisy, and reasoning is brittle. We present WebExpert, a domain-aware web agent that we implement end-to-end, featuring : (i) sentence-level experience retrieval with topic merging and rule distillation, (ii) schemalight facet induction that bootstraps time,region,policy,industry facets from weak supervision instead of static hand-written lexicons, and (iii) preference-optimized planning that jointly improves query planning and retrieval via pairwise preference learning alongside a coverage-aware objective. At inference, a lightweight experience gate biases decoding toward active facets with fallback under low-retrieval confidence. On GAIA, GPQA, HLE, and WebWalkerQA, WebExpert improves Answer Exact Match (EM) by 1.5-3.6 pp over the strongest browsing baseline and reduces page hops. Analysis shows consistent gains and ablations on retrieval, topic merging, facet induction, and preference-aware training.

</details>


### [176] [ARIA: Adaptive Retrieval Intelligence Assistant -- A Multimodal RAG Framework for Domain-Specific Engineering Education](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06179)
*Yue Luo,Dibakar Roy Sarkar,Rachel Herring Sangree,Somdatta Goswami*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出ARIA框架，一种基于检索增强生成(RAG)的智能教学助手系统，通过多模态内容提取和领域自适应机制，在工程专业课程中实现97.5%的问题过滤准确率和4.89/5.0的回答质量，解决了通用大模型在专业教育场景中的幻觉和领域知识不足问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用大语言模型在专业教育应用中存在显著局限性，包括幻觉现象、知识更新受限和领域专业知识缺乏。传统微调方法计算成本高昂，而依赖通用训练数据的模型在专业场景中常提供不准确回答，亟需构建既能保证教学准确性又具备领域适应性的教育AI系统。

Method: 提出ARIA（自适应检索智能助手）框架，采用检索增强生成(RAG)架构。核心是多模态内容提取管道：结合Docling进行结构化文档分析、Nougat识别数学公式、GPT-4 Vision API解析图表，并使用e5-large-v2嵌入模型实现高语义性能与低延迟。通过工程化提示词和响应控制机制维持教学一致性。

Result: 在约翰霍普金斯大学土木工程专业大二课程"静力学与材料力学"的评估中，ARIA表现优异：领域问题过滤准确率97.5%，正确回答全部20个相关课程问题，拒绝60个非相关问题中的58个，精确率90.9%，召回率100%，平均回答质量达4.89/5.0，显著优于ChatGPT-5。

Conclusion: ARIA的课程无关架构证明了其在专业教育AI部署中的可扩展性，为构建准确、可靠的领域特定教学助手提供了可扩展框架，有效平衡了专业知识的准确性与系统的适应性。

Abstract: Developing effective, domain-specific educational support systems is central to advancing AI in education. Although large language models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable capabilities, they face significant limitations in specialized educational applications, including hallucinations, limited knowledge updates, and lack of domain expertise. Fine-tuning requires complete model retraining, creating substantial computational overhead, while general-purpose LLMs often provide inaccurate responses in specialized contexts due to reliance on generalized training data. To address this, we propose ARIA (Adaptive Retrieval Intelligence Assistant), a Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) framework for creating intelligent teaching assistants across university-level courses. ARIA leverages a multimodal content extraction pipeline combining Docling for structured document analysis, Nougat for mathematical formula recognition, and GPT-4 Vision API for diagram interpretation, with the e5-large-v2 embedding model for high semantic performance and low latency. This enables accurate processing of complex educational materials while maintaining pedagogical consistency through engineered prompts and response controls. We evaluate ARIA using lecture material from Statics and Mechanics of Materials, a sophomore-level civil engineering course at Johns Hopkins University, benchmarking against ChatGPT-5. Results demonstrate 97.5% accuracy in domain-specific question filtering and superior pedagogical performance. ARIA correctly answered all 20 relevant course questions while rejecting 58 of 60 non-relevant queries, achieving 90.9% precision, 100% recall, and 4.89/5.0 average response quality. These findings demonstrate that ARIA's course-agnostic architecture represents a scalable framework for domain-specific educational AI deployment.

</details>


### [177] [The Unreasonable Effectiveness of Data for Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06420)
*Youssef Abdou*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模实证研究探讨推荐系统中训练数据量与离线性能的关系，发现增加数据量通常持续提升NDCG@10性能，未观察到饱和点，表明更多训练数据对传统推荐系统仍主要有益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推荐系统中大规模交互数据的收集、存储和处理成本日益增高，但额外数据何时停止带来有意义增益尚不明确。研究数据量增加对离线推荐性能的影响及是否存在饱和点，对优化资源配置和成本控制具有重要意义。

Method: 研究构建了可复现的Python评估流程，采用LensKit和RecBole两个工具包，在11个至少包含700万条交互的大型公开数据集上，评估10种工具-算法组合。通过绝对分层用户采样，在10万至1亿条交互的九个样本规模上训练模型，以NDCG@10为评估指标，并进行了组内最小-最大归一化和后期斜率分析。

Result: 原始NDCG随样本量增加通常持续上升，未发现明显饱和点。经组内最小-最大归一化后，最大完成样本量处约75%的观测点达到组内最佳性能。后期斜率分析（每组最后10-30%）显示四分位距完全非负，中位数接近1.0。较差的扩展行为集中在非典型案例及RecBole BPR算法中。

Conclusion: 对于传统推荐系统和典型用户-项目交互数据，纳入更多训练数据仍主要带来性能提升，支持在推荐系统实践中继续扩展训练数据的价值。但需注意在特定数据集和算法（如RecBole BPR）上可能观察到较弱的扩展行为。

Abstract: In recommender systems, collecting, storing, and processing large-scale interaction data is increasingly costly in terms of time, energy, and computation, yet it remains unclear when additional data stops providing meaningful gains. This paper investigates how offline recommendation performance evolves as the size of the training dataset increases and whether a saturation point can be observed. We implemented a reproducible Python evaluation workflow with two established toolkits, LensKit and RecBole, included 11 large public datasets with at least 7 million interactions, and evaluated 10 tool-algorithm combinations. Using absolute stratified user sampling, we trained models on nine sample sizes from 100,000 to 100,000,000 interactions and measured NDCG@10. Overall, raw NDCG usually increased with sample size, with no observable saturation point. To make result groups comparable, we applied min-max normalization within each group, revealing a clear positive trend in which around 75% of the points at the largest completed sample size also achieved the group's best observed performance. A late-stage slope analysis over the final 10-30% of each group further supported this upward trend: the interquartile range remained entirely non-negative with a median near 1.0. In summary, for traditional recommender systems on typical user-item interaction data, incorporating more training data remains primarily beneficial, while weaker scaling behavior is concentrated in atypical dataset cases and in the algorithmic outlier RecBole BPR under our setup.

</details>


### [178] [CASE: Cadence-Aware Set Encoding for Large-Scale Next Basket Repurchase Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06718)
*Yanan Cao,Ashish Ranjan,Sinduja Subramaniam,Evren Korpeoglu,Kaushiki Nag,Kannan Achan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出CASE模型，通过日历时间信号和多尺度时序卷积显式建模商品复购节奏，在公共数据集和生产环境上均显著超越现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有购物篮推荐模型将历史表示为按访问顺序离散的篮子事件序列，无法显式建模购买间隔的日历时间信息，也无法在两次购买之间的天数流逝时更新商品排序。针对频繁补货类目的复购推荐，这种时序建模缺陷限制了预测准确性。

Method: CASE（Cadence-Aware Set Encoding）模型将商品级节奏学习与商品间交互解耦。具体包括：1）将每个商品的购买历史表示为固定时间跨度内的日历时间信号；2）应用共享的多尺度时序卷积捕捉周期性复购规律；3）使用诱导集注意力机制以亚二次复杂度建模商品间依赖关系，实现大规模高效批量推理。

Result: 在三个公开基准数据集和专有数据集上，CASE在多个截断位置的Precision、Recall和NDCG指标上持续优于强基线模型。在生产环境评估中，面对数千万用户和大规模商品库，CASE在top-5推荐上实现了高达8.6%的相对Precision提升和9.9%的Recall提升。

Conclusion: 显式的日历时间建模与可扩展的节奏感知表示学习，在基准测试和工业场景下均带来可量化的性能增益，证明了CASE方法的有效性。

Abstract: Repurchase behavior is a primary signal in large-scale retail recommendation, particularly in categories with frequent replenishment: many items in a user's next basket were previously purchased and their timing follows stable, item-specific cadences. Yet most next basket repurchase recommendation models represent history as a sequence of discrete basket events indexed by visit order, which cannot explicitly model elapsed calendar time or update item rankings as days pass between purchases. We present CASE (Cadence-Aware Set Encoding for next basket repurchase recommendation), which decouples item-level cadence learning from cross-item interaction, enabling explicit calendar-time modeling while remaining production-scalable. CASE represents each item's purchase history as a calendar-time signal over a fixed horizon, applies shared multi-scale temporal convolutions to capture recurring rhythms, and uses induced set attention to model cross-item dependencies with sub-quadratic complexity, allowing efficient batch inference at scale. Across three public benchmarks and a proprietary dataset, CASE consistently improves Precision, Recall, and NDCG at multiple cutoffs compared to strong next basket prediction baselines. In a production-scale evaluation with tens of millions of users and a large item catalog, CASE achieves up to 8.6% relative Precision and 9.9% Recall lift at top-5, demonstrating that scalable cadence-aware modeling yields measurable gains in both benchmark and industrial settings.

</details>


### [179] [Leveraging LLMs and Heterogeneous Knowledge Graphs for Persona-Driven Session-Based Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06928)
*Muskan Gupta,Suraj Thapa,Jyotsana Khatri*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于异构知识图谱的用户画像驱动会话推荐框架，通过两阶段架构显式建模潜在用户画像并融入推荐流程，在Amazon数据集上性能优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统会话推荐系统因匿名会话假设而在数据稀疏和冷启动场景下个性化能力受限。尽管LLM能生成丰富的商品表示，但匿名会话下用户画像建模仍具挑战。本文旨在突破此限制，显式建模从异构知识图谱推断的潜在用户画像并整合至推荐流程。

Method: 采用两阶段架构：1) 个性化信息抽取：构建融合用户-商品、商品-商品、商品-特征关联及DBpedia元数据的异构知识图谱，利用基于LLM商品嵌入初始化的异构图深度信息最大化（HDGI）目标无监督学习潜在用户画像；2) 个性化信息利用：将学得的用户画像表示与LLM商品嵌入共同输入改进的会话推荐架构生成候选集，再通过基础序列模型重排序以强化短期会话意图。

Result: 在Amazon Books和Amazon Movies & TV数据集上的实验表明，该方法相较于仅使用会话历史生成用户嵌入的序列模型，性能持续提升。

Conclusion: 该方法通过知识图谱的结构化关系信号为用户画像建模提供可解释基础，区别于单纯依赖序列建模或文本表示的现有方法，有效提升了会话推荐在稀疏和冷启动场景下的个性化能力。

Abstract: Session-based recommendation systems (SBRS) aim to capture user's short-term intent from interaction sequences. However, the common assumption of anonymous sessions limits personalization, particularly under sparse or cold-start conditions. Recent advances in LLM-augmented recommendation have shown that LLMs can generate rich item representations, but modeling user personas with LLMs remains challenging due to anonymous sessions. In this work, we propose a persona-driven SBRS framework that explicitly models latent user personas inferred from a heterogeneous knowledge graph (KG) and integrates them into a data-driven recommendation pipeline.Our framework adopts a two-stage architecture consisting of personalized information extraction and personalized information utilization, inspired by recent chain-of-thought recommendation approaches. In the personalized information extraction stage, we construct a heterogeneous KG that integrates time-independent user-item, item-item, item-feature association, and metadata from DBpedia. We then learn latent user personas in an unsupervised manner using a Heterogeneous Deep Graph Infomax (HDGI) objective over a KG initialized with LLM-derived item embeddings. In the personalized information utilization stage, the learned persona representations together with LLM-derived item embeddings are incorporated into a modified architecture of data-driven SBRS to generate a candidate set of relevant items, followed by reranking using the base sequential model to emphasize short-term session intent. Unlike prior approaches that rely solely on sequence modeling or text-based user representations, our method grounds user persona modeling in structured relational signals derived from a KG. Experiments on Amazon Books and Amazon Movies & TV demonstrate that our approach consistently improves over sequential models with user embeddings derived using session history.

### [180] [MARVEL: Multimodal Adaptive Reasoning-intensiVe Expand-rerank and retrievaL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07079)
*Mahmoud SalahEldin Kasem,Mohamed Mahmoud,Mostafa Farouk Senussi,Mahmoud Abdalla,Abdelrahman Abdallah,Hyun-Soo Kang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对多模态检索效果不佳的问题，本文提出MARVEL统一框架，结合LLM查询扩展、推理增强的密集检索器和GPT-4o思维链重排序，在MM-BRIGHT基准上达到37.9 nDCG@10，显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言编码器在多模态检索基准MM-BRIGHT上表现仅27.6 nDCG@10，低于纯文本系统，且现有方法孤立处理查询扩展、复杂推理检索和重排序三个关键能力，缺乏统一框架。

Method: MARVEL采用三阶段统一流程：1) LLM驱动查询意图扩展；2) MARVEL-Retriever（推理增强的密集检索器，针对复杂多模态查询微调）；3) GPT-4o思维链重排序，可选多轮互反排序融合。

Result: 在涵盖29个技术领域的MM-BRIGHT基准上，MARVEL达到37.9 nDCG@10，比最佳多模态编码器提升+10.3分，在27个领域超越所有单阶段基线，在剩余两个高度专业化领域（密码学、量子计算）接近最佳基线。

Conclusion: 推理密集型多模态检索需要通过统一扩展-检索-重排序框架来解决，MARVEL证明了这一方法的有效性，显著提升了多模态检索性能。

Abstract: Multimodal retrieval over text corpora remains a fundamental challenge: the best vision-language encoder achieves only 27.6 nDCG@10 on MM-BRIGHT, a reasoning-intensive multimodal retrieval benchmark, underperforming strong text-only systems. We argue that effective multimodal retrieval requires three tightly integrated capabilities that existing approaches address only in isolation: expanding the query's latent intent, retrieving with a model trained for complex reasoning, and reranking via explicit step-by-step reasoning over candidates. We introduce \textbf{MARVEL} (\textbf{M}ultimodal \textbf{A}daptive \textbf{R}easoning-intensi\textbf{V}e \textbf{E}xpand-rerank and retrieva\textbf{L}), a unified pipeline that combines LLM-driven query expansion, \textbf{MARVEL-Retriever} -- a reasoning-enhanced dense retriever fine-tuned for complex multimodal queries -- and GPT-4o-based chain-of-thought reranking with optional multi-pass reciprocal rank fusion. Evaluated on MM-BRIGHT across 29 technical domains, MARVEL achieves \textbf{37.9} nDCG@10, surpassing the best multimodal encoder by \textbf{+10.3 points} and outperforming all single-stage baselines in 27 of 29 domains and matching or approaching the best baseline in the remaining two highly-specialized domains (Crypto, Quantum Computing), demonstrating that reasoning-intensive multimodal retrieval is best addressed through a unified expand-retrieve-rerank framework. https://github.com/mm-bright/multimodal-reasoning-retrieval

### [181] [BRIDGE: Multimodal-to-Text Retrieval via Reinforcement-Learned Query Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07201)
*Mohamed Darwish Mounis,Mohamed Mahmoud,Shaimaa Sedek,Mahmoud Abdalla,Mahmoud SalahEldin Kasem,Abdelrahman Abdallah,Hyun-Soo Kang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对多模态图文查询在纯文本语料库检索中的性能瓶颈问题，本文提出BRIDGE系统，通过FORGE模型将含噪多模态查询精炼为优化检索字符串，配合LENS推理增强检索器，在MM-BRIGHT数据集上达到29.7 nDCG@10，证明查询对齐是关键瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言编码器在多模态到文本检索任务中表现不佳（MM-BRIGHT上仅27.6 nDCG@10），作者认为瓶颈不在于检索器，而在于原始多模态查询中视觉描述、对话噪声与检索意图的纠缠会系统性地降低嵌入相似度，导致检索性能下降。

Method: 提出两组件系统BRIDGE：1) FORGE（专注检索查询生成器）：通过强化学习训练查询对齐模型，将噪声多模态查询提炼为紧凑的检索优化字符串；2) LENS（语言增强神经搜索）：在推理密集型检索数据上微调的推理增强稠密检索器，用于处理FORGE生成的意图丰富查询。

Result: 在MM-BRIGHT（2,803个查询，29个领域）上，BRIDGE达到29.7 nDCG@10，超越所有多模态编码器基线。当FORGE作为即插即用对齐器与Nomic-Vision结合时，系统达到33.3 nDCG@10，超过最佳纯文本检索器（32.2），提升显著。

Conclusion: 研究表明多模态到文本检索的核心瓶颈是查询对齐而非检索模型本身。通过有效的查询精炼和对齐，多模态查询可以转化为高质量文本查询，从而使现有文本检索系统性能大幅提升，为多模态检索提供了新思路。

Abstract: Multimodal retrieval systems struggle to resolve image-text queries against text-only corpora: the best vision-language encoder achieves only 27.6 nDCG@10 on MM-BRIGHT, underperforming strong text-only retrievers. We argue the bottleneck is not the retriever but the query -- raw multimodal queries entangle visual descriptions, conversational noise, and retrieval intent in ways that systematically degrade embedding similarity. We present \textbf{BRIDGE}, a two-component system that resolves this mismatch without multimodal encoders. \textbf{FORGE} (\textbf{F}ocused Retrieval Query Generato\textbf{r}) is a query alignment model trained via reinforcement learning, which distills noisy multimodal queries into compact, retrieval-optimized search strings. \textbf{LENS} (\textbf{L}anguage-\textbf{E}nhanced \textbf{N}eural \textbf{S}earch) is a reasoning-enhanced dense retriever fine-tuned on reasoning-intensive retrieval data to handle the intent-rich queries FORGE produces. Evaluated on MM-BRIGHT (2,803 queries, 29 domains), BRIDGE achieves \textbf{29.7} nDCG@10, surpassing all multimodal encoder baselines including Nomic-Vision (27.6). When FORGE is applied as a plug-and-play aligner on top of Nomic-Vision, the combined system reaches \textbf{33.3} nDCG@10 -- exceeding the best text-only retriever (32.2) -- demonstrating that \textit{query alignment} is the key bottleneck in multimodal-to-text retrieval. https://github.com/mm-bright/multimodal-reasoning-retrieval

### [182] [HIVE: Query, Hypothesize, Verify An LLM Framework for Multimodal Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07220)
*Mahmoud Abdalla,Mahmoud SalahEldin Kasem,Mohamed Mahmoud,Mostafa Farouk Senussi,Abdelrahman Abdallah,Hyun-Soo Kang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对多模态检索模型在需要深度视觉-文本推理的查询上表现不佳的问题，本文提出HIVE框架，通过LLM驱动的假设生成与验证，在MM-BRIGHT数据集上实现41.7 nDCG@10，显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态检索模型在处理需要深度整合图像（图表、截图等）与文本的推理密集型查询时表现不佳，最佳多模态模型在MM-BRIGHT上仅达27.6 nDCG@10，甚至低于纯文本检索器（32.2），存在明显的多模态推理差距。

Method: 提出HIVE（假设驱动迭代视觉证据检索）框架，包含四个阶段：1）初始检索；2）基于LLM的补偿性查询合成，显式识别top-k候选中的视觉与逻辑缺口；3）使用优化查询进行二次检索；4）LLM验证并重新排序候选集。该框架可与标准或推理增强的检索器即插即用。

Result: 在MM-BRIGHT多模态到文本赛道（2,803个真实查询，29个技术领域）上，HIVE取得41.7 nDCG@10的新SOTA结果，较最佳纯文本模型提升+9.5，较最佳多模态模型提升+14.1。基础推理增强检索器贡献33.2分，HIVE框架额外增加+8.5分，在视觉需求高的领域表现尤为突出（游戏：68.2，化学：42.5，可持续：49.4）。

Conclusion: LLM介导的视觉假设生成与验证能显著缩小检索中的多模态推理差距，HIVE框架验证了该方法的有效性，为多模态检索提供了新的解决思路。

Abstract: Multimodal retrieval models fail on reasoning-intensive queries where images (diagrams, charts, screenshots) must be deeply integrated with text to identify relevant documents -- the best multimodal model achieves only 27.6 nDCG@10 on MM-BRIGHT, underperforming even strong text-only retrievers (32.2). We introduce \textbf{HIVE} (\textbf{H}ypothesis-driven \textbf{I}terative \textbf{V}isual \textbf{E}vidence Retrieval), a plug-and-play framework that injects explicit visual-text reasoning into a retriever via LLMs. HIVE operates in four stages: (1) initial retrieval over the corpus, (2) LLM-based compensatory query synthesis that explicitly articulates visual and logical gaps observed in top-$k$ candidates, (3) secondary retrieval with the refined query, and (4) LLM verification and reranking over the union of candidates. Evaluated on the multimodal-to-text track of MM-BRIGHT (2,803 real-world queries across 29 technical domains), HIVE achieves a new state-of-the-art aggregated nDCG@10 of \textbf{41.7} -- a \textbf{+9.5} point gain over the best text-only model (DiVeR: 32.2) and \textbf{+14.1} over the best multimodal model (Nomic-Vision: 27.6), where our reasoning-enhanced base retriever contributes 33.2 and the HIVE framework adds a further \textbf{+8.5} points -- with particularly strong results in visually demanding domains (Gaming: 68.2, Chemistry: 42.5, Sustainability: 49.4). Compatible with both standard and reasoning-enhanced retrievers, HIVE demonstrates that LLM-mediated visual hypothesis generation and verification can substantially close the multimodal reasoning gap in retrieval. https://github.com/mm-bright/multimodal-reasoning-retrieval

</details>
